/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[buspaciente]    Script Date: 05/07/2014 06:47:42 p.m. ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

create PROCEDURE [dbo].[buspaciente]
    
 
	
  

AS
BEGIN

    SET NOCOUNT ON;

    Begin Tran Tadd

    Begin Try
	select (e.idPaciente) as codigo, concat(p.pnombrePer,' ',p.snombrePer) as nombre,concat(p.pApellPer,' ',p.sApellPer) as apellido  from persona as p inner join paciente as e on e.fkpersona=p.idPersona; 
   

        COMMIT TRAN Tadd

    End try
    Begin Catch

     
        Rollback TRAN Tadd

    End Catch

END



GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[buspacientedocu]    Script Date: 05/07/2014 06:47:42 p.m. ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

create PROCEDURE [dbo].[buspacientedocu]
    
 @numDocu as varchar(50)
	
  

AS
BEGIN

    SET NOCOUNT ON;

    Begin Tran Tadd

    Begin Try
	select (e.idPaciente) as codigo, concat(p.pnombrePer,' ',p.snombrePer) as nombre,concat(p.pApellPer,' ',p.sApellPer) as apellido  from persona as p inner join paciente as e on e.fkpersona=p.idPersona inner join documento as do on p.idPersona=do.fkpersona where do.numero=@numDocu  ;
   

        COMMIT TRAN Tadd

    End try
    Begin Catch

     
        Rollback TRAN Tadd

    End Catch

END



GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[InsertCita]    Script Date: 05/07/2014 06:47:42 p.m. ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
Create procedure [dbo].[InsertCita](@idHorario int, @fechaCita date, @idMedicoAsig int, @idPaciente int, @idPersona int, @MotivoCita varchar(50), @CorreoPaciente varchar(50), @Telefono varchar(50))
as
Insert into cita(fechaCita, correoCita,motivo, estadoCita, fkhorario, fkPaciente) values(@fechaCita,@CorreoPaciente,@MotivoCita, 'sin confirmacion',@idHorario, @idPaciente)
Insert into correo(Correo,fkPersona) values(@CorreoPaciente,@idPersona)
Insert into telefono(numero,tipo,idPerson)values(@Telefono,'residencial',@idPersona)



GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[PacienteConfirmado]    Script Date: 05/07/2014 06:47:42 p.m. ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[PacienteConfirmado]
   


AS
BEGIN

    SET NOCOUNT ON;

    Begin Tran Tadd

    Begin Try
select (c.idCita)as Codigo, concat(p.pnombrePer,'',p.snombrePer,'' ,p.pApellPer,'',p.sApellPer) as nombre,(c.motivo)Motivo,(g.nombreCargo)Especialidad,(m.pApellPer ) as Medico,(h.horaini)as Hora from cita as c inner join paciente as a on c.fkPaciente=a.idPaciente
inner join persona as p on p.idPersona=a.fkpersona
inner join horario as h on h.idhorario=c.fkhorario
inner join empleado as e on e.idEmpleado=h.fkempleado
inner join persona as m on e.fkpersona=m.idPersona
inner join cargo as g on g.idCargo=e.fkCargo where c.fechaCita=CONVERT (date, GETDATE()) and c.estadoCita='confirmado' and h.horaini>=convert(time,GETDATE()) ;

        COMMIT TRAN Tadd

    End try
    Begin Catch

       
        Rollback TRAN Tadd

    End Catch

END



GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[PacienteEspera]    Script Date: 05/07/2014 06:47:42 p.m. ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[PacienteEspera]
   
  

AS
BEGIN

    SET NOCOUNT ON;

    Begin Tran Tadd

    Begin Try

  select (c.idCita)as Codigo, c.correoCita,(p.pnombrePer) as Nombre,(c.fechacita) as FechaSolicitud ,convert(date,getdate()) as Fecha,(h.horaini)as Hora,( c.estadoCita) as Estado from cita as c inner join paciente as a on c.fkPaciente=a.idPaciente
inner join persona as p on p.idPersona=a.fkpersona
inner join horario as h on h.idhorario=c.fkhorario
inner join empleado as e on e.idEmpleado=h.fkempleado
inner join persona as m on e.fkpersona=m.idPersona
inner join cargo as g on g.idCargo=e.fkCargo where c.estadoCita='espera' and fechaCita>=CONVERT(date,getdate()) ;

        COMMIT TRAN Tadd

    End try
    Begin Catch

       
        Rollback TRAN Tadd

    End Catch

END



GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[PacienteTarde]    Script Date: 05/07/2014 06:47:42 p.m. ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[PacienteTarde]
   


AS
BEGIN

    SET NOCOUNT ON;

    Begin Tran Tadd

    Begin Try
select (c.idCita)as Codigo,concat(p.pnombrePer,' ',p.snombrePer,' ' ,p.pApellPer,' ',p.sApellPer) as nombre,(m.pApellPer ) as Medico from cita as c inner join paciente as a on c.fkPaciente=a.idPaciente
inner join persona as p on p.idPersona=a.fkpersona
inner join horario as h on h.idhorario=c.fkhorario
inner join empleado as e on e.idEmpleado=h.fkempleado
inner join persona as m on e.fkpersona=m.idPersona
inner join cargo as g on g.idCargo=e.fkCargo where c.fechaCita=CONVERT (date, GETDATE()) and c.estadoCita='confirmado' and h.horaini<convert(time,GETDATE()) ;

        COMMIT TRAN Tadd

    End try
    Begin Catch

       
        Rollback TRAN Tadd

    End Catch

END



GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[registroempleado]    Script Date: 05/07/2014 06:47:42 p.m. ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[registroempleado]
    @rol as int,
    @usu AS VARCHAR(50),
    @pass AS VARCHAR(50),
    @pnombre AS VARCHAR(30),
	@snombre AS VARCHAR(30),
	@papellido AS VARCHAR(30),
	@sapellido AS VARCHAR(30),
	@fechanaci AS date,
	@sexo AS VARCHAR(2),
	
	@numDocu as varchar(50),
    @tipodocu as varchar(50),
	@numtele as varchar(50),
	@tipotele as varchar(50),
	@calle as varchar(50),
	@casa as varchar(50),
	@munici as int,
	@correo as varchar(50),
	@tipocorreo as varchar(50),
    
	@cargo as int,
	@tipoempleado as int,
    @idpersona as int=0

AS
BEGIN

    SET NOCOUNT ON;

    Begin Tran Tadd

    Begin Try

        INSERT INTO dbo.login(usuLogin,passLogin,fkRol) VALUES (@usu,@pass,@rol)
        INSERT INTO dbo.persona(pnombrePer,snombrePer,pApellPer,sApellPer,fechaNacPer,sexo,fkLogin) VALUES (@pnombre,@snombre,@papellido,@sapellido,@fechanaci,@sexo,@@IDENTITY)
		select @idpersona=@@IDENTITY
	    INSERT INTO  dbo.documento(numero,tipo,fkpersona ) values (@numDocu,@tipodocu,@idpersona)
		INSERT INTO  dbo.telefono(numero,tipo,idPerson) values(@numtele,@tipotele,@idpersona)
		INSERT INTO dbo.Direccion(calleDireccion,casaDireccion,fkMunicipio,fkpersona)values(@calle,@casa,@munici,@idpersona)
		INSERT INTO  dbo.correo(Correo,tipo,fkPersona) values(@correo,@tipocorreo,@idpersona)
		insert into dbo.empleado(fkCargo,fkTipoemple,fkpersona) values(@cargo,@tipoempleado,@idpersona)
     

        COMMIT TRAN Tadd

    End try
    Begin Catch

        
        Rollback TRAN Tadd

    End Catch

END



GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[registroUsuario]    Script Date: 05/07/2014 06:47:42 p.m. ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[registroUsuario]
    @usu AS VARCHAR(50),
    @pass AS VARCHAR(50),
    @pnombre AS VARCHAR(30),
	@snombre AS VARCHAR(30),
	@papellido AS VARCHAR(30),
	@sapellido AS VARCHAR(30),
	@fechanaci AS date,
	@sexo AS VARCHAR(2),
    @igle AS VARCHAR(50),
	@numDocu as varchar(50),
    @tipodocu as varchar(50),
	@numtele as varchar(50),
	@tipotele as varchar(50),
	@calle as varchar(50),
	@casa as varchar(50),
	@munici as int,
	@correo as varchar(50),
	@tipocorreo as varchar(50),
   
    @idpersona as int=0
  

AS
BEGIN

    SET NOCOUNT ON;

    Begin Tran Tadd

    Begin Try

        INSERT INTO dbo.login(usuLogin,passLogin,fkRol) VALUES (@usu,@pass,1)
        INSERT INTO dbo.persona(pnombrePer,snombrePer,pApellPer,sApellPer,fechaNacPer,sexo,fkLogin,iglesia) VALUES (@pnombre,@snombre,@papellido,@sapellido,@fechanaci,@sexo,@@IDENTITY,@igle)
		select @idpersona=@@IDENTITY
	    INSERT INTO  dbo.documento(numero,tipo,fkpersona ) values (@numDocu,@tipodocu,@idpersona)
		INSERT INTO  dbo.telefono(numero,tipo,idPerson) values(@numtele,@tipotele,@idpersona)
		INSERT INTO dbo.Direccion(calleDireccion,casaDireccion,fkMunicipio,fkpersona)values(@calle,@casa,@munici,@idpersona)
		INSERT INTO  dbo.correo(Correo,tipo,fkPersona) values(@correo,@tipocorreo,@idpersona)
		insert into dbo.paciente(fkpersona) values(@idpersona)
   

        COMMIT TRAN Tadd

    End try
    Begin Catch

     
        Rollback TRAN Tadd

    End Catch

END



GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[responsable]    Script Date: 05/07/2014 06:47:42 p.m. ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
create PROCEDURE [dbo].[responsable]
    
 
	
  

AS
BEGIN

    SET NOCOUNT ON;

    Begin Tran Tadd

    Begin Try
	select p.idpaciente,  n.pnombrePer,n.snombrePer,n.pnombrePer,n.sApellPer from paciente as p inner join persona as n on n.idPersona=p.fkpersona
   

        COMMIT TRAN Tadd

    End try
    Begin Catch

     
        Rollback TRAN Tadd

    End Catch

END



GO

/****** Object:  Trigger [dbo].[tEntrada]    Script Date: 05/07/2014 06:47:43 p.m. ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

  Create trigger [dbo].[tEntrada]
   on [dbo].[entrada]
   for Insert
   as

   Update m set m.existenciaMedica=m.existenciaMedica + cantidadEntrada
   from medicamento as m inner join
   INSERTED as D on D.fkMedicamento=m.idMedica


GO
